### [1] [A Viscosity Semigroup Framework for Stable Image Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20620)
*Arina Oberoi*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文在黏性解框架下建立了退化椭圆-抛物型偏微分方程驱动的多尺度图像表示理论，并基于该理论设计了一种结合学习型逆映射与非线性扩散演化的混合重建算子，在CT间皮瘤分类任务中验证了该方法的稳定性优势。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有的多尺度图像表示方法缺乏严格的数学基础，尤其是在退化椭圆-抛物型偏微分方程框架下的适定性分析尚不完善；同时，学习驱动的重建方法往往缺乏稳定性保证，难以在实际应用中实现可靠的收敛行为。

**Method:** 从尺度空间理论的公理化表述出发，在黏性解框架下利用比较原理建立了退化椭圆-抛物型PDE的适定性、唯一性和上确界范数压缩性；在此基础上提出混合重建算子，先由学习型逆映射进行初始重建，再经由非线性扩散演化进行后处理，该扩散算子在连续层面上满足非扩张性从而保证稳定性。

**Result:** 在CT间皮瘤分类任务中，所提方法AUC达0.875且跨epoch波动极小，而基线模型AUC在0.49至0.80间大幅波动且无明确收敛趋势，实验结果与黏性理论所预示的稳定化作用一致。

**Conclusion:** 黏性解框架为退化椭圆-抛物型PDE驱动的图像表示提供了严格的适定性基础，混合重建算子的稳定性来源于扩散算子的非扩张性，该理论-实践结合的策略为医学图像等高精度任务提供了一种鲁棒且可解释的建模路径。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Starting from the axiomatic formulation of scale-space theory, we develop a viscosity-solution framework for multiscale image representations arising from degenerate elliptic-parabolic partial differential equations. Rather than introducing a new semigroup theory, we work within the standard viscosity-solution setting, using comparison principles to obtain well-posedness, uniqueness, and contraction in the supremum norm. This perspective is used to motivate a hybrid reconstruction operator in which a learned inverse map is followed by a nonlinear diffusion evolution. At the continuous level, the diffusion operator satisfies non-expansiveness, which provides stability for the reconstruction process; this framework is then evaluated on a CT-based mesothelioma classification task, where it attains an AUC of 0.875 with negligible variation across epochs, while the baseline model acquires AUC values from 0.49 to 0.80 without a clear convergence pattern. These observations are consistent with the stabilizing role suggested by the discussed viscosity theory.


### [2] [NeoJaundice-AI: Smartphone-Based Neonatal Jaundice Detection Using Dual-Input Deep Learning and Synthetic Augmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20689)
*Rahul Patel, Nirjala Jarpula*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出NeoJaundice-AI，一个基于智能手机的新生儿黄疸筛查系统，采用双分支EfficientNet-B0架构融合皮肤与巩膜图像及手工YCbCr颜色特征，结合合成黄疸数据生成方法和肤色归一化模块，实现四分类严重度评估和连续胆红素回归预测，在离线移动端达到91.8%分类准确率、93.5%临床灵敏度和1.4 mg/dL胆红素平均绝对误差。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 新生儿黄疸（高胆红素血症）影响全球新生儿，印度每年约1500万例，早期检测至关重要但标准血液检测在农村诊所因实验室设施不足而难以实施，现有方法缺乏针对印度深肤色人群（Fitzpatrick IV–VI型）的适配，且严重黄疸病例数据稀少。

**Method:** 系统采用双分支EfficientNet-B0架构分别处理皮肤和巩膜图像，将深度特征与手工提取的YCbCr颜色统计特征融合，同时执行四类严重度分类和连续胆红素回归；提出合成黄疸生成方法，通过可控YCbCr通道修改在正常新生儿皮肤图像上模拟胆红素诱导的黄染以缓解数据稀缺；引入肤色归一化模块提升跨肤色预测一致性；最终经过INT8量化和ONNX转换将模型压缩至8.3 MB并实现离线移动端部署。

**Result:** 整体分类准确率达91.8%，临床灵敏度为93.5%，胆红素平均绝对误差为1.4 mg/dL；模型经INT8量化与ONNX转换后大小降至8.3 MB，在标准Android设备上推理时间低于3秒。

**Conclusion:** 该工作首次在统一框架中结合多模态图像融合、肤色自适应、合成数据增强和完全离线移动部署，为印度及类似资源受限地区提供了一种实用、快速且低成本的新生儿黄疸筛查方案。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Neonatal jaundice (hyperbilirubinemia) is one of the most common conditions affecting newborns worldwide, with India alone recording roughly 15 million cases per year. Early detection is critical, yet standard diagnosis requires blood tests that are often impractical in rural clinics where laboratory facilities are limited. This paper presents NeoJaundice-AI, a smartphone-based screening system that uses photographs of a baby's skin and sclera (eye white) to estimate jaundice severity and predict serum bilirubin levels in under three seconds without requiring internet connectivity.
  The proposed system is built on a dual-branch EfficientNet-B0 architecture that independently processes skin and sclera images. Deep features are fused with handcrafted YCbCr color statistics to jointly perform four-class severity classification and continuous bilirubin regression. A key contribution is a synthetic jaundice generation method that simulates bilirubin-induced yellowing through controlled YCbCr channel modifications on normal neonatal skin images. This approach addresses data scarcity, particularly for severe jaundice cases and darker Indian skin tones (Fitzpatrick Types IV to VI). In addition, a skin-tone normalization module improves prediction consistency across diverse neonatal complexions.
  Experimental results demonstrate an overall classification accuracy of 91.8 percent, a clinical sensitivity of 93.5 percent, and a bilirubin mean absolute error of 1.4 mg/dL. After INT8 quantization and ONNX conversion, the model size is reduced to 8.3 MB while maintaining inference times below three seconds on standard Android devices. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first India-focused neonatal jaundice AI system that combines multimodal image fusion, skin-tone adaptation, synthetic data augmentation, and fully offline mobile deployment within a single framework.


### [3] [AEF-Econ: Toward Plug-and-Play Socioeconomic Foundation Embeddings from AlphaEarth for Urban Remote Sensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20697)
*Shuyang Hou, Ziqi Liu, Haoyue Jiao, Lutong Xie, Yaxian Qing, Xiaopu Zhang, Qingyang Xu, Zhangyan Xu, Xuefeng Guan, Huayi Wu*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出Capacity-Adaptive Reconstruction (CAR)方法，解决了多模态社会经济遥感基础嵌入中高维流抑制低维流的问题，将跨区域R²从0.301提升至0.848，并构建了CHN-Econ基准和AEF-Econ嵌入集。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有AlphaEarth Foundations (AEF) 的遥感基础嵌入聚焦于物理地表信号，难以直接用于社会经济任务；同时，多模态社会经济数据融合中存在高维嵌入流在共享重构中抑制低维语义流的能力竞争问题，导致部分标签预测失效。

**Method:** 首先整合七类异构数据（AEF嵌入、人口、夜间灯光、遥感指数、POI、城市形态、跨语言文本）构建CHN-Econ基准；沿五个轴线（融合架构、自监督目标、文本整合、嵌入维度、归一化）进行31项控制实验；提出Capacity-Adaptive Reconstruction (CAR)，以每流独立解码器和逐流损失替代共享重构，缓解流间容量竞争。

**Result:** AEF线性探针在跨区域和跨层级评估中仅达R²=0.301和0.160；五轴消融主干将指标提升至0.832和0.671；CAR进一步将跨区域和跨层级R²提升至0.848和0.693，并将负R²标签恢复至稳定范围；最终推断36城市8年1440万像素，发布128d和64d压缩版AEF-Econ。

**Conclusion:** CAR有效解决了多模态社会经济融合中的流间容量竞争问题；AEF-Econ在无监督下捕获跨城市层级与城内空间组织，作为社会经济遥感基础嵌入与AEF物理嵌入互补；低维语义流在多模态融合中需专门的解耦策略以避免被高维流支配。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
AlphaEarth Foundations (AEF) unify global remote sensing foundation embeddings through multimodal self-supervised learning, but their pretraining focuses on physical land-surface signals, limiting plug-and-play use in socioeconomic tasks. We integrate seven heterogeneous data streams across 36 Chinese cities over eight years - AEF embeddings, population, nighttime lights, remote sensing indices, points of interest (POIs), urban morphology, and cross-lingual text - and construct CHN-Econ, a socioeconomic benchmark with 16 labels in three categories. We conduct 31 controlled experiments along five axes: fusion architecture, self-supervised objective, text integration, embedding dimensionality, and normalization. Used alone as a linear probe, AEF achieves R2 values of only 0.301 for cross-region and 0.160 for cross-tier evaluation. The five-axis ablated backbone improves these scores to 0.832 and 0.671, respectively, but reveals that low-dimensional semantic streams are consistently suppressed by high-dimensional streams under shared reconstruction. To address this bottleneck, we propose Capacity-Adaptive Reconstruction (CAR), replacing shared reconstruction with per-stream decoders and stream-level losses to mitigate inter-stream capacity competition. CAR further raises cross-region and cross-tier R2 to 0.848 and 0.693, and restores collapsed labels from negative R2 to a stable range. Using CAR, we infer 14.4 million pixels across 36 cities and eight years and release AEF-Econ, including 128d and 64d compressed versions. Self-diagnostics and case studies show that AEF-Econ captures cross-city hierarchies and intra-urban spatial organization under unsupervised settings, providing a socioeconomic remote sensing foundation embedding complementary to AEF physical embeddings.


### [4] [Beyond Templates: Revisiting Zero-Shot Remote Sensing through Meta-Prompting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20702)
*Eirini Baltzi, Dionysis Christopoulos, Sotiris Spanos, Valsamis Ntouskos, Konstantinos Karantzalos*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文系统评估了17种VLM变体在12个遥感数据集上的零样本性能，发现LLM生成的语义丰富描述在文本嵌入空间中引入噪声，反而不如简单的领域适配CLIP描述鲁棒，并提出轻量级查询嵌入校准方法可显著提升零样本分类与检索性能。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 尽管视觉-语言模型在零样本遥感下游任务中展现出潜力，且遥感适配模型进一步提升了性能，但零样本性能对文本设计选择（包括元提示和类别描述）高度敏感，LLM生成的语义丰富描述并不能稳定带来性能增益，甚至可能引入噪声降低鲁棒性，亟需系统研究描述语义丰富性与下游任务鲁棒性之间的权衡关系。

**Method:** 采用元提示视觉识别（MPVR）框架，在17种VLM变体和12个遥感数据集上进行系统评估；通过白化CLIP特征空间中的文本对数似然分析，比较LLM生成描述与模板基描述的嵌入质量；进一步提出轻量级查询嵌入校准方法，对查询空间进行校准以提升零样本分类和检索性能。

**Result:** 实验表明LLM生成的类别描述虽语义表达更丰富，但在文本嵌入空间中会引入噪声，导致下游任务鲁棒性下降；基于白化CLIP特征空间的文本对数似然分析验证了该发现；轻量级查询嵌入校准能在零样本分类和检索任务上持续带来显著的性能提升。

**Conclusion:** 本研究揭示了遥感零样本任务中语义丰富性与鲁棒性之间的关键权衡，指出嵌入校准是一种简单有效的性能提升工具，为实际部署中文本描述策略的选择提供了实用指导。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Vision-language models (VLMs) have sparked growing interest in zero-shot Earth Observation (EO) downstream tasks, with further gains enabled by remote-sensing-adapted models. We examine this setting across 17 VLM variants and 12 remote sensing (RS) datasets under Meta-Prompting for Visual Recognition (MPVR), and show that zero-shot performance remains highly sensitive to textual design choices, from the meta-prompts used to guide the LLM in generating class descriptions to the descriptions themselves. We explore why semantically rich LLM-generated class descriptions do not translate into consistent gains over simple domain-adapted CLIP-style descriptions. While LLM descriptions are more semantically expressive, they can also introduce noise in the text embedding space, reducing robustness in downstream tasks. We support this observation through a text log-likelihood analysis in the whitened CLIP feature space, comparing LLM-generated and template-based descriptions. Building on this finding, we study query embedding calibration and show that lightweight calibration of the query space consistently yields strong improvements in zero-shot classification and retrieval. Overall, our results provide practical insight into the trade-off between semantic richness and robustness, and identify embedding calibration as a simple and effective tool for improving zero-shot remote sensing performance.


### [5] [TeleStyle V2: Beyond Content-Preserving Style Transfer with Self-Distillation and Distribution-Matching-Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20709)
*Shiwen Zhang, Yifan Xu, Haibin Huang, Chi Zhang, Xuelong Li*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
TeleStyle V2 提出了自蒸馏数据合成策略和分布匹配蒸馏（DMD）方法，突破了TeleStyle V1仅支持写实内容+艺术风格的局限，实现了四种内容-风格参考组合（RnR/RnS/SnR/SnS）的风格迁移，并在通用图像编辑能力上与Qwen-Image-Edit和Gemini-3-pro等模型持平或更优。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** TeleStyle V1仅支持写实内容参考与艺术风格参考的组合，无法处理艺术内容参考与写实风格参考等更多样化的组合场景，并且存在内容/风格参考顺序混淆问题及微调导致的内容一致性退化问题。

**Method:** 提出自蒸馏数据合成策略，利用TeleStyle V1为任意内容-风格参考组合构建三元组训练数据；引入分布匹配蒸馏（Distribution Matching Distillation, DMD）以保持基础模型原有的文本引导图像编辑能力并修复SFT导致的内容一致性退化；采用Qwen2.5-VL-7B作为VLM编码器自动生成内容提示和风格提示，并引入提示增强器解决参考顺序混淆问题。

**Result:** TeleStyle V2-QIE-2509-DMD在性能上与Qwen-Image-Edit-2509-DMD至少持平，展现出超越内容保留风格迁移的强通用图像编辑能力；同时与商业SOTA模型Gemini-3-pro-image-preview相比取得可比的风格迁移性能。

**Conclusion:** 自蒸馏数据合成策略有效拓展了风格迁移的适用参考组合范围，分布匹配蒸馏在保持基础模型通用编辑能力方面具有关键作用，提示增强器解决了顺序混淆问题，证明了模型在风格迁移与通用图像编辑任务上的统一潜力。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Given a content reference and a style reference, content-preserving style transfer requires the model to generate stylized outputs with content and style consistency. We introduced TeleStyle V1 to tackle this problem. However, TeleStyle V1 is trained with photorealistic content reference and artistic style reference, which makes it incapable to cope with artistic content reference and realistic style reference in most cases. In this paper, we designed a Self-Distillation data synthesis strategy to construct such triplets from TeleStyle V1. Trained with such self-distilled triplets, our TeleStyle V2 supports Content-Style references in the forms of Realistic-and-Realistic (RnR), Realistic-and-Stylized (RnS), Stylized-and-Realistic (SnR), Stylized-and-Stylized (SnS). In addition, we found Distribution Matching Distillation could preserve the general text-guided image editing capability of the foundation model and fix the content consistency degradation caused by SFT process. Through quantitative evaluations, our TeleStyleV2-QIE-2509-DMD performs at least on par with Qwen-Image-Edit-2509-DMD, demonstrating strong general image editing skills beyond content-preserving style transfer. We observed the content/style reference order confusion problem in TeleStyle V1 and further introduced prompt enhancer to solve it. TeleStyle V2 uses Qwen-Image-Edit's VLM encoder, Qwen2.5-VL-7B, to generate content prompt and style prompt for free. TeleStyle V2 could achieve comparable style transfer performance with state-of-the-art commercial model, gemini-3-pro-image-preview.


### [6] [Video2Code: Generating Interactive Webpages from UI Videos via Action-Aware Revisit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20711)
*Mingde Xu, Zhen Yang, Yan Wang, Yu Wang, Xijun Liu, Zijun Dou, Wenyi Hong, Xiaotao Gu, Bin Xu, Jie Tang*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
Video2Code提出了一种动作感知的UI视频到代码生成方法，通过先粗粒度定位动作关键区域，再以更高时间分辨率重新采样这些区域，从而解决现有视频模型因稀疏采样导致的状态-动作-状态转换对齐问题，显著提升了多步交互场景下的功能正确性。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有视频视觉语言模型在将UI视频直接转换为可交互网页时，通常依赖稀疏采样或压缩时域表示，这容易遗漏短暂的动作边界，破坏了实现网页行为所需的状态-动作-状态转换。论文将此问题形式化为状态-转换不对齐（state-transition misalignment），并针对性地提出解决方案。

**Method:** Video2Code首先对整个视频进行粗粒度理解以定位动作关键区域（action-critical regions），然后调用时域裁剪工具（temporal clipping tool）对这些区域以更高时间分辨率重新采样，从而在不增加全局视觉预算的前提下获取精细的动作边界信息，最后基于增强后的视觉表示生成HTML/CSS/JavaScript代码，并以动作对齐的视频-代码监督进行实例化训练。

**Result:** 实验表明Video2Code在UI视频到代码生成任务上显著提升了底层开源模型的能力，在视觉和功能双重评估标准下，特别是在密集多步交互场景中，功能正确性（functional correctness）相比直接使用完整视频观测的方法有实质性提高。

**Conclusion:** 该工作揭示了视频模型在UI转代码任务中由于时域采样导致的状态转换丢失问题，并提出了一种动作感知的粗到细采样策略来有效恢复可执行的UI状态转换，为从自然交互视频生成功能性网页提供了新的技术路径。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
UI videos provide a natural input for generating interactive webpages, as they capture both webpage appearance and action-triggered state transitions. However, directly applying video-capable vision-language models to this task remains insufficient. Existing models typically rely on sparse sampling or compressed temporal representations, which may miss short action boundaries and break the state-action-state transitions needed to implement webpage behavior. We formulate UI video-to-code generation as executable state-transition recovery from interaction videos, and identify this failure mode as state-transition misalignment. We introduce Video2Code, an action-aware video-to-code approach for recovering executable UI state transitions. Rather than allocating the visual budget uniformly across the video, Video2Code first performs coarse video understanding to locate action-critical regions, then invokes a temporal clipping tool to revisit these regions at higher temporal resolution before generating HTML/CSS/JavaScript code. We instantiate Video2Code with action-aligned video-code supervision and evaluate it under both visual and functional criteria. Experiments show that Video2Code substantially strengthens the underlying open-source model for UI video-to-code generation, improving functional correctness over direct video observation, especially on dense multi-step interactions.


### [7] [MIRAGE: Stealthy Visual Prompt Injection for Vulnerability Detection in Web Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20717)
*Xuelong Dai, Jianyu Ma, Boyang Ma, Biwei Yan, Yijun Yang, Yue Zhang*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
MIRAGE提出了一种在受信任网页平台上，仅通过控制语义合法且空间受限区域（如广告位）进行视觉间接提示注入攻击的新框架，利用扩散模型生成感知无害的对抗性图像，实现对MLLM网页代理的下一动作劫持。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有针对MLLM网页代理的对抗性评估通常依赖宽松的威胁模型和视觉上明显的伪造痕迹，缺乏对现实受限场景（如攻击者仅能控制广告位等合法区域）下视觉漏洞的系统研究。

**Method:** 提出MIRAGE框架，采用扩散模型生成严格限制在受信任服务提供商允许边界内的感知良性对抗图像；引入曲率感知对抗扩散引导与稀疏暗像素残差扰动相结合的鲁棒优化技术，在高度约束条件下最大化攻击效能。

**Result:** 在SeeAct和OpenClaw两个主流MLLM网页代理框架上的全面评估，实证证明了MIRAGE在攻击效能、真实性和隐蔽性方面的显著优势。

**Conclusion:** 该研究揭示了MLLM网页代理在现实受限威胁模型下存在严重的视觉安全漏洞，为后续防御机制的研究提供了新的攻击基准和风险评估视角。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Multimodal Large Language Model (MLLM)-based web agents provide practical, high-precision solutions for visual browser automation; however, they inherently expand the attack surface, introducing novel vision-based vulnerabilities. Existing adversarial evaluations targeting these agents frequently rely on permissive threat models and visually conspicuous artifacts. In this paper, we investigate a constrained vulnerability detection setting: a trusted web platform where the evaluator acts solely as an unprivileged third party, such as a merchant or advertiser, controlling only a semantically legitimate, spatially constrained region, such as an ad slot, a sponsored card, or a localized widget. Operating under these realistic constraints, we propose MIRAGE, a novel visual indirect prompt injection framework for targeted next-action hijacking. Our approach leverages diffusion models to generate perceptually benign adversarial images strictly confined to the attacker-controlled boundaries permitted by the trusted service provider. To maximize attack efficacy within such a restrictive setting, we introduce a robust optimization technique combining curvature-aware adversarial diffusion guidance with sparse, dark-pixel residual perturbations. Comprehensive evaluations against prominent MLLM web agent frameworks, specifically SeeAct and OpenClaw, empirically demonstrate the potency, realism, and stealth of our proposed MIRAGE.


### [8] [Evaluation of Medical Vision Language Models HuluMed and MedGemma, and general purpose chatbots Gemma 3, ChatGPT Plus, and Claude Pro on real previously unseen wound images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20723)

#### 📘 Detailed Summary

**Conclusion:** 前沿通用型多模态系统在伤口分析性能上显著优于医学专用替代模型，凸显了广泛多模态推理能力与医学领域知识相结合的重要性；当前VLM在临床决策支持方面展现出潜力，但在高级伤口管理推理、程序规划和自主临床可靠性方面仍存在显著局限。

#### 📄 Abstract
Chronic wound assessment remains a clinically challenging task that requires accurate interpretation of wound morphology, tissue composition, vascular characteristics, and infection risk. Recent advances in Vision-Language Models (VLMs) have introduced the possibility of automated multimodal wound analysis through image understanding combined with clinical reasoning. This study evaluates the performance of several general-purpose and medically specialized open-source and proprietary VLMs for clinical wound assessment using an expanded, curated dataset of 20 clinically diverse wounds spanning vascular, surgical, ischemic, venous, lymphedema, and amputation-related etiologies. Six VLMs were evaluated using a structured twelve-question clinical framework covering wound classification, infection risk, vascular intervention recommendations, debridement urgency, wound therapy selection, and advanced management planning. Across 20 wound cases and 240 clinician-graded wound-analysis decisions, ChatGPT achieved the highest overall performance with 174/240 correct responses (72.50%), followed by Claude with 149/240 (62.08%). Among the open-source and medically specialized models, HuluMed achieved the strongest performance with 96/240 correct responses (40.00%), followed by Gemma 3 (81/240, 33.75%), MedGemma 4B (62/240, 25.83%), and MedGemma 27B (42/240, 17.50%). The findings suggest that frontier general-purpose multimodal systems currently demonstrate substantially stronger wound-analysis performance than medically specialized alternatives, highlighting the continued importance of broad multimodal reasoning capabilities alongside domain-specific medical knowledge. Although current VLMs demonstrate promising potential for clinical decision support, substantial limitations remain in advanced wound-management reasoning, procedural planning, and autonomous clinical reliability.


### [9] [How Well Can Your Video Model Remember? Measuring Memory-Budget Trade-offs in Long Video Understanding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20726)
*Yixian Tian*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
该论文提出了一个关于长视频理解中答案准确率随帧预算B和时间距离D衰减的实证模型，发现logit-准确率与log-预算呈线性关系，且距离相关指数α(D)随距离对数线性衰减；不同模型在长距离下的预算效率差异显著（如STREAMINGVLM的α(1000)为1.26，而Qwen3-VL仅为0.17），并提出α(D)作为流式视频模型的诊断指标与预算分配工具。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 长视频理解模型在严格帧预算下运行，但现有研究缺乏一个能够预测答案准确率如何随帧预算减少和事件时间距离增加而退化的量化框架，无法为模型比较和预算分配提供理论指导。

**Method:** 作者基于约155,000个二元预测样本（涵盖十种模型和三种采样策略），采用加权最小二乘法拟合了一个紧凑的经验模型，其中logit-准确率与log-预算呈线性关系，其斜率（预算指数α(D））随时间距离D呈对数线性衰减，从而量化了不同距离下额外帧的边际价值。

**Result:** 该模型在cell级别上实现加权R²范围为0.05-0.75；在D=1000秒处，流式模型STREAMINGVLM的预算指数α(1000)=1.26（95% CI: [1.06, 1.58]），而最佳基座模型Qwen3-VL仅为α(1000)=0.17（CI: [0.04, 0.34]），预算效率差异约7.4倍；10倍预算增加在D=1000秒时分别带来+29个百分点与+4个百分点的准确率提升；采样策略呈现模型依赖性的权衡关系。

**Conclusion:** α(D)能够实现原则性的预算分配，揭示长期距离下的模型排名反转现象，并可作为流式视频模型的诊断指标，为长视频理解中的资源效率评估与模型选择提供了理论工具。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
We introduce a compact empirical model that quantifies how answer accuracy degrades as a function of frame budget B and temporal distance D in long video understanding -- analyzing performance when recalling content from D seconds in the past using a fraction B of total frames. Long-form models operate under strict budgets, yet no prior framework predicts how accuracy degrades as B shrinks and events recede. We fit a weighted least-squares model on ~155,000 binary predictions across ten models and three sampling strategies, deriving a law where logit-accuracy scales linearly in log-budget with a distance-dependent exponent that decays log-linearly with distance. This budget exponent α(D) captures the marginal value of extra frames at distance D. The law achieves cell-level weighted R^2 = 0.05-0.75 across models. Notably, budget effectiveness at D = 1000 s differs by \approx 7.4\times between the best streaming and base models. STREAMINGVLM achieves α(1000) = 1.26 (95% CI: [1.06, 1.58]), meaning a tenfold budget increase substantially improves long-distance accuracy, while the best Qwen3-VL base model reaches only α(1000) = 0.17 (CI: [0.04, 0.34]). In accuracy space, a 10\times budget increase at D = 1000 s yields +29 percentage points for STREAMINGVLM versus +4 pp for the base model. Sampling strategies show model-dependent trade-offs: random sampling yields higher base sensitivity but steeper distance decay. We demonstrate how α(D) enables principled budget allocation, including a model-ranking reversal at long distance, and propose it as a diagnostic metric for streaming video models.


### [10] [VTOS: Learning to Orchestrate Vision Tools by Co-Searching Solutions and Observers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20728)
*Jinchao Ge, Lingqiao Liu, Shuwen Zhao, Lei Wang*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
VTOS 提出联合搜索解决方案程序与观察者程序的框架，通过共享的 VisionThoughts 知识库迭代诊断与反馈，在密集目标计数和零样本植物病害分割任务上超越静态流水线与现有智能体编程基线。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有视觉编程智能体通常生成固定的解决方案流水线，在密集目标、遮挡、小目标和域迁移等视觉条件下表现脆弱，缺乏对视觉工具编排（包括工具选择、顺序、参数和视觉条件）的自适应调整能力。

**Method:** VTOS 提出联合搜索框架，同步搜索可执行的解决方案程序（编排 Grounding DINO、SAM、NMS、slice-and-detect 等视觉工具）与观察者程序（诊断候选方案、识别失败模式并生成可操作反馈），并将观测结果累积到共享的 VisionThoughts 知识库中以指导后续搜索过程。

**Result:** 在密集目标计数任务（LVIS-Count）和零样本植物病害分割任务（PlantSeg-OOD）上，VTOS 均优于静态工具流水线和现有的智能体视觉编程基线，验证了联合搜索解决方案与观察者在阈值校准、NMS、切片、掩码精化和域泛化等编排挑战上的有效性。

**Conclusion:** 联合搜索解决方案与观察者是一种有效的策略，能够使视觉工具自适应地应对具有挑战性的计算机视觉任务，其核心在于通过共享知识库积累观测反馈来迭代优化工具编排策略。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Vision foundation tools such as open-vocabulary detectors, segmentation models, and post-processing operators are powerful building blocks for computer vision, but their effectiveness depends heavily on how they are orchestrated: which tools are used, in what order, with what parameters, and under what visual conditions. Existing visual-programming agents typically generate a fixed solution pipeline, making them brittle under dense objects, occlusion, small targets, and domain shift. We introduce VTOS (Vision Tools Orchestration Search), a framework for adaptive visual tool orchestration through joint solution--observer search. VTOS co-searches executable solution programs that compose vision tools such as Grounding DINO, SAM, NMS, and slice-and-detect, together with observer programs that diagnose candidate solutions, identify failure modes, and generate actionable feedback. These observations are accumulated in a shared VisionThoughts knowledge base to guide subsequent search. We evaluate VTOS through two case studies: dense object counting on LVIS-Count and zero-shot plant-disease segmentation on PlantSeg-OOD, which stress different orchestration challenges including threshold calibration, NMS, slicing, mask refinement, and domain generalization. Across both tasks, VTOS outperforms static tool pipelines and agentic visual-programming baselines, showing that co-searching solutions and observers is an effective strategy for adapting vision tools to challenging computer vision tasks.


### [11] [REKEY: Metadata-Grounded Visual-Key Regeneration for Contamination-Resilient VQA Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20736)
*Tengjie Lin, Yutao Sun, Jingwei Ni, Shuhan Ge, Hao-Xuan Ma, Yanting Miao, Wangyue Lu, Mingshuai Chen, Tiancheng Zhao, Jianwei Yin*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
提出ReKey协议，通过在评测时随机重新生成图像中的局部视觉关键区域，使VQA基准测试具备动态更新能力，避免静态基准因数据泄露导致的记忆化问题。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 静态VQA基准会因数据泄露而迅速过时，模型得分可能反映的是记忆而非真实视觉理解能力，而人工重建高质量基准成本高昂且同样面临泄露风险。

**Method:** ReKey是一种实时基准测试协议，利用人工验证的编辑槽位在评测时随机重新生成真实图像中承载答案的局部视觉关键区域，每次采样生成新实例、新答案、构造标签并控制视觉搜索难度。

**Result:** 在V*Bench上应用ReKey后，8个前沿视觉语言模型在原始数据上的得分比重新生成变体高出9.5至18.8个百分点，揭示了显著的记忆化效应。

**Conclusion:** 通过使视觉关键区域可更新，ReKey能够在模型与训练数据持续演进的过程中保持评测的新鲜度和有效性，为动态、防泄露的VQA评测提供了可行范式。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Static visual question answering (VQA) benchmarks age quickly: Once the items leak into training corpora, scores can reflect memorization rather than genuine visual ability, thus obscuring real progress. Rebuilding high-quality benchmarks such as V*Bench requires substantial human annotation, yet each static release can quickly become another leaked artifact. We propose ReKey, a live benchmark protocol that randomly regenerates the answer-bearing local detail, or visual key, in real images at evaluation time. Using human-validated edit slots, ReKey samples fresh instances with new answers, construction-grounded labels, and controlled visual-search difficulty. On V*Bench, the ReKey regenerated benchmark reveals a sharp score jump across eight frontier vision-language models (VLMs): The original items score 9.5--18.8 percentage points higher than the regenerated variants. By making the visual key renewable, ReKey keeps evaluation fresh as models and training data evolve.


### [12] [Mirage: a Clean-Label Backdoor against LiDAR 3D Object Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20752)
*Ziba Parsons, Ang Li*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
Mirage是一种针对基于深度神经网络的LiDAR 3D目标检测模型的黑盒、干净标签后门攻击方法，通过在训练集中注入少量标签一致的毒化样本，使模型将特定触发模式与攻击者选择的类别关联起来，在仅0.5%的投毒率下实现73%的错误分类成功率，同时保持与良性模型相近的检测性能。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有针对LiDAR 3D目标检测的后门攻击通常需要白盒访问或修改标签，且主要集中于物体消失或边界框操纵等几何攻击，缺乏对更隐蔽、更实用的黑盒且无需标签修改攻击场景的研究。

**Method:** Mirage提出了一种黑盒且干净标签的后门攻击方法，通过在训练集中注入少量标签一致的毒化样本，使模型学习触发模式与攻击者选择的目标类别之间的恶意关联，同时保持正常训练语义；被感染的模型在正常输入上表现正常，但在部署阶段会将带有触发器的物体系统性错误分类为目标类别。

**Result:** 在多个最先进的LiDAR 3D目标检测模型和基准数据集上的实验表明，Mirage在仅0.5%的投毒率下即可达到73%的错误分类成功率，同时检测性能与良性模型相近。

**Conclusion:** Mirage证明了在LiDAR 3D目标检测中存在一种更隐蔽、更具实用性的后门攻击风险，即攻击者无需白盒访问或标签修改即可有效破坏模型的安全性，揭示了安全关键自动驾驶系统中的潜在威胁。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Deep neural network-based LiDAR 3D object detection serves as a critical perception component in safety-critical autonomous systems. However, recent studies have revealed its vulnerability to backdoor attacks. Existing attacks typically require white-box access or label modification and focus on geometric attacks such as object disappearance or bounding-box manipulation. In this paper, we present Mirage, a black-box and clean-label backdoor attack against deep neural network-based LiDAR 3DOD. Mirage injects a small number of label-consistent poisoning samples into the training set, causing the model to learn a malicious association between a trigger pattern and an attacker-chosen target class while preserving normal training semantics. As a result, the compromised model behaves normally on benign inputs yet systematically misclassifies triggered objects as the target class during deployment. We evaluate Mirage on multiple state-of-the-art LiDAR 3DOD models and benchmark datasets. Experimental results show that Mirage achieves a 73% misclassification success rate with a poisoning rate of only 0.5%, while maintaining detection performance close to that of benign models.


### [13] [One Image is All You Need: Agentic One-Shot Image Generation via Text-Based World Models for Long-Tail Spatial Perception](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20764)
*Keqin Zeng, Shuting Su, Shihao Lin, Ziyue Li, Rui Zhao*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
WMGen-v1 提出基于智能体文本化世界模型的框架，通过 LVLM 构建结构化场景表示、LLM 进行引导式场景扩展，再以扩散模型生成物理合理的长尾空间数据，仅用合成数据训练检测器即可接近真实数据性能，有效缓解时空感知中的长尾数据稀缺问题。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 自动驾驶、海事监控等空间决策系统依赖鲁棒的视觉感知，但真实时空数据存在严重异质性，安全关键场景呈现极端长尾分布，导致数据集偏移、检测性能下降及安全隐患；现有合成数据生成方法（扩散模型、GAN）缺乏显式空间约束和物理一致性，生成场景存在空间与物理上的不一致性。

**Method:** WMGen-v1 是一个智能体文本化世界模型框架：首先利用大型视觉语言模型（LVLM）从单张参考图像构建结构化场景表示，然后借助大型语言模型（LLM）在物理合理性和常识约束下进行引导式场景扩展，最后将推理生成的结构化语义表示作为条件输入扩散模型，生成多样化且物理合理的长尾训练数据。

**Result:** 在内部工业数据集、ROADWork 和 LaRS 基准上，WMGen-v1 在检测性能上优于基线方法；值得注意的是，仅使用 WMGen-v1 合成数据训练的检测器在聚合数据集级别指标上接近真实数据训练的性能，证明了其在缓解下游空间感知任务长尾数据稀缺方面的有效性。

**Conclusion:** WMGen-v1 通过将 LVLM 和 LLM 的结构化推理能力与扩散模型的生成能力相结合，实现了物理可解释的长尾空间数据生成，为减轻现实世界中安全关键场景的数据稀缺问题提供了可行路径，对自动驾驶、海事监控等领域的可靠空间决策具有重要实际意义。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Reliable spatial decision automation, such as autonomous driving and maritime surveillance, critically depends on robust visual perception. However, real-world spatiotemporal data exhibits severe heterogeneity, often manifesting as extreme long-tail distributions for safety-critical scenarios. This data scarcity induces dataset shift that degrades detection performance and pose safety risks. While synthetic data generation offers a potential solution, existing generative approaches, such as diffusion models and Generative Adversarial Networks (GANs), often lack explicit spatial grounding and structural constraints, resulting in spatial and physical inconsistencies in generated scenes. To address these challenges, we introduce WMGen-v1, an agentic text-based world model framework for long-tail spatial data generation. WMGen-v1 employs a Large Vision-Language Model (LVLM) to construct a structured scene representation from a single reference image, while a Large Language Model (LLM) performs guidance-based scene expansion under physical plausibility and commonsense constraints. Subsequently, conditioned on the structured semantic representations produced by this reasoning process, a diffusion model generates diverse and physically grounded long-tail training data. Experiments on internal industrial datasets, ROADWork, and LaRS benchmarks demonstrate that WMGen-v1 outperforms baseline approaches. Notably, detectors trained solely on WMGen-v1 synthetic data approach real-only performance on aggregate dataset-level metrics, highlighting its potential to alleviate long-tail data scarcity for downstream spatial perception.


### [14] [Translating Inference-Time Control to Radiology Vision-Language Models: Activation Steering for Pneumonia Classification on Chest X-rays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20852)
*Eduardo Moreno Judice de Mattos Farina, Mateus A. Esmeraldo, Felipe Akio Matsuoka, Paulo Eduardo de Aguiar Kuriki, Felipe Campos Kitamura*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文系统评估了对比激活添加（CAA）方法在无需微调的情况下通过推理时工程提升胸部X光片视觉语言模型（VLM）肺炎分类性能的效果，结果表明CAA能显著改变预测得分分布，并在三个评估VLM中的一个（NV-Reason-CXR-3B）上实现了有意义的性能提升，校准F1从0.7692提升至0.8727。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 推理时工程可以在不进行微调的情况下改变模型行为，但其在医疗视觉语言模型（VLM）中改善诊断性能的实用性尚不清楚，本研究旨在评估对比激活添加（CAA）方法在无需更新模型权重的情况下改善胸部X光片VLM肺炎分类性能的有效性。

**Method:** 使用三种冻结权重的胸部X光片VLM（MedGemma-4B-IT、NV-Reason-CXR-3B和CheXOne-3B）在公开的Kermany肺炎测试集上进行评估，分类基于二元提示下Yes和No标记的对数几率（logits）；构建了三种引导向量：30对答案偏置控制向量、30对肺炎文本对比向量以及基于图像条件的对比向量（由30张肺炎和30张正常发育图像衍生而来）；使用200张确定性发育集进行层和尺度选择（100张）及阈值校准（100张），性能评估指标包括ROC-AUC、PR-AUC、F1分数、阈值分析、反向向量控制、随机向量控制及条件自助法置信区间。

**Result:** 固定阈值F1改善虽频繁出现但并未一致反映诊断性能提升；NV-Reason-CXR-3B表现出最显著的收益，校准F1从零样本的0.7692提升至肺炎文本引导下的0.8619和图像条件引导下的0.8727；CheXOne-3B的肺炎文本引导使校准F1从0.8528提升至0.8666，但置信区间跨越零；总体而言，CAA显著改变了预测得分分布和操作特性，但在三个评估VLM中仅有一个实现了有意义的性能增益。

**Conclusion:** 对比激活添加（CAA）作为一种轻量级的推理时干预方法，能够显著改变医疗VLM的预测行为，但对诊断性能的提升因模型而异，在部分模型上效果有限；激活引导可能作为一种无需微调的轻量级方法来适应医疗VLM的行为，但其适用性和可靠性需要进一步验证。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Inference-time engineering can alter model behavior without fine-tuning. However, its utility for improving diagnostic performance in medical vision-language models (VLMs) remains unclear. We aim to evaluate whether Contrastive Activation Addition (CAA) can improve pneumonia classification in chest radiograph VLMs without updating model weights. Three frozen chest radiograph VLMs (MedGemma-4B-IT, NV-Reason-CXR-3B, and CheXOne-3B) were evaluated on the public Kermany pneumonia test set. Classification was based on the logits of the tokens Yes and No under a binary prompt. Steering vectors included a 30-pair answer-bias control, a 30-pair pneumonia text contrast, and an image-conditioned contrast derived from 30 pneumonia and 30 normal development images. A deterministic 200-image development set was used for layer and scale selection (100 images) and threshold calibration (100 images). Performance was assessed using ROC-AUC, PR-AUC, F1 score, threshold analyses, reverse-vector controls, random-vector controls, and conditional bootstrap confidence intervals. Fixed-threshold F1 improvements were frequently observed but did not consistently indicate improved diagnostic performance. For MedGemma-4B-IT. NV-Reason-CXR-3B showed the strongest benefit: calibrated F1 improved from 0.7692 in the zero-shot setting to 0.8619 with pneumonia-text steering and to 0.8727 with image-conditioned steering. For CheXOne-3B, pneumonia-text steering increased calibrated F1 from 0.8528 to 0.8666, although the confidence interval crossed zero. On this public pneumonia benchmark, CAA substantially altered prediction score distributions and operating characteristics without fine-tuning. Meaningful performance gains were observed in one of three evaluated VLMs, suggesting that activation steering may serve as a lightweight approach for adapting medical VLM behavior.


### [15] [Toward Parking Spot Occupancy Recognition: A Self-Supervised Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20886)
*Luan Marko Kujavski, Rayson Laroca, Paulo Lisboa de Almeida*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
提出一种两阶段自监督训练策略，结合SimCLR和ResNet-50，在无需目标停车场标注数据的情况下实现车位占用识别，平均准确率达97.8%。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有停车场车位占用识别方法通常依赖大量有标注数据，难以在无标注的新目标停车场上直接部署，限制了系统的可扩展性和实际落地应用。

**Method:** 采用基于SimCLR和ResNet-50编码器的自监督对比学习框架，训练策略包含两个自监督阶段（先在通用无标注数据上预训练，再在目标领域无标注数据上继续自监督训练），最后仅使用通用停车场标注数据进行有监督微调；同时提出两阶段部署策略：先部署强通用模型，再利用部署前N天收集的无标注图像通过自监督方式得到专用模型。

**Result:** 在PKLot、CNRPark-EXT和PLds三个公开数据集上采用留一法跨环境评估，强通用模型平均准确率达97.2%，超越现有监督和自监督基线；两阶段策略进一步提升至97.8%。

**Conclusion:** 自监督学习能够实现无需目标标注的可扩展车位占用识别方案，为实际停车场监控提供了高效、低成本且易于部署的解决方案。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
As urban areas expand, automatic monitoring of parking lots becomes essential for efficient and sustainable cities. This work proposes a self-supervised approach for parking spot occupancy recognition that requires no labeled samples from the target parking lot. Building upon a self-supervised transfer learning fine-tuning protocol, the proposed training strategy consists of two self-supervised stages: first on unlabeled generic data and then on unlabeled target-specific data, followed by supervised fine-tuning using only generic parking lot labels. We adopt SimCLR with a ResNet-50 encoder and evaluate the method under a leave-one-out cross-environment protocol on three public datasets: PKLot, CNRPark-EXT, and PLds. We also introduce a two-stage deployment strategy in which a Strong General Model is initially deployed, followed by a Specialized Model that incorporates unlabeled images collected during the first N days of deployment in a self-supervised manner. Experimental results show that the Strong General Model alone outperforms supervised and self-supervised baselines, achieving an average accuracy of 97.2%, which further improves to 97.8% with the proposed two-stage strategy. These results demonstrate that self-supervised learning enables a scalable and labelefficient solution for real-world parking occupancy monitoring. Our trained models and source code are publicly available at https://github.com/LoanMaikon/Parking-Spot-Occupancy-Recognition.


### [16] [Go-with-the-Track: Video Compositing and Motion Control with Point Tracking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20891)
*Koichi Namekata, Yash Kant, Zhizheng Liu, Ryan D Burgert, Yuancheng Xu, Kuan Heng Lin, Emmett Steven, Julien Philip, Li Ma, Andrea Vedaldi, Paul Debevec, Ning Yu*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
Go-with-the-Track提出了一种统一参考图像合成与点轨迹运动控制的方法，通过引入参考锚定点轨迹（reference-anchored point-tracks）建立生成帧与参考图像之间的显式对应关系，并采用空间感知点轨迹嵌入与轻量级适配器注入视频扩散Transformer，在单个模型中实现了比现有方法更优的运动与参考控制以及多参考条件视频生成等新能力。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有方法将电影制作所需的精确运动控制与参考图像合成能力割裂处理：点轨迹条件图像到视频模型将内容插入限制在首帧，而参考到视频模型缺乏对参考内容在帧间融合方式的细粒度时空控制，因此需要一种统一两种能力的框架。

**Method:** 提出参考锚定点轨迹，将常规点轨迹扩展为显式建立生成帧与参考图像之间的对应关系；设计空间感知点轨迹嵌入，通过坐标级MLP和时序池化编码完整点轨迹坐标序列，使嵌入相似度直接与空间邻近性相关；通过轻量级适配器将点轨迹嵌入注入视频扩散Transformer，解决像素到patch的分辨率失配问题并避免朴素下采样带来的运动细节丢失；采用混合训练策略，联合动态、静态和合成场景视频数据集进行训练以增强运动可控性。

**Result:** 实验表明Go-with-the-Track在单一模型中实现了优于现有方法的运动控制和参考控制，并支持多项新能力：多参考条件视频生成与点轨迹驱动的合成、以及静态与动态场景的相机控制。

**Conclusion:** 该研究通过统一参考图像合成与点轨迹运动控制，为电影级视频生成提供了更灵活且精确的解决方案，并展示了在多种复杂视频生成任务上的广泛适用性。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Filmmaking demands precise motion control and reference image compositing -- capabilities that existing methods treat separately. Point-track-conditioned image-to-video models restrict content insertion to the first frame, while reference-to-video models lack fine-grained spatial-temporal control over how reference content integrates across frames.
  We present Go-with-the-Track, which unifies both capabilities by jointly conditioning on multiple reference images and reference-anchored point-tracks -- extending conventional point-tracks to explicitly establish correspondences between generated frames and reference images, thus enabling precise compositing and motion control throughout the video.
  To achieve this, we introduce spatially-aware point-track embeddings that encode the full sequence of point-track coordinates using a coordinate-wise MLP followed by temporal pooling. This representation captures the spatial characteristics of each point-track (serving as a unique identifier), while the embedding similarity correlates directly with spatial proximity, enhancing the model's ability to distinguish and associate point-tracks. We inject these point-track embeddings into a video diffusion transformer via a lightweight adapter, resolving the pixel-to-patch resolution mismatch while avoiding the substantial motion detail loss inherent in naive point-track subsampling.
  We use a hybrid training strategy to train jointly on dynamic, static, and synthetic scene video datasets to boost motion controllability. Experiments demonstrate that Go-with-the-Track achieves superior motion and reference control in a single model and enables new capabilities: multi-reference conditioned video generation with point-track driven compositing, as well as camera control for both static and dynamic scenes. Project Page: https://eyeline-labs.github.io/Go-with-the-Track/


### [17] [BELDE: Building a Large-scale Earth-observation Land-cover Dataset for Europe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20909)
*Ümit Mert Çağlar, Alptekin Temizel*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
BELDE是一个面向欧洲的10米分辨率RGB遥感土地覆盖分割大规模公开数据集，包含超108万对图像-标注图，涵盖7类地物，并在跨地域泛化实验中揭示了显著的地理域偏移挑战（欧洲F1达83.0%，而美国及韩国分别降至66.4%和58.3%）。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有土地覆盖分割数据集在地理覆盖范围、规模和公开可访问性方面存在局限，而多光谱数据虽日益普及，但受限于成本和部署条件，真彩色RGB影像仍然是卫星与航空遥感平台中的主流数据形式，亟需一个大规模、标准化且公开的RGB遥感分割基准以支持模型开发和跨区域泛化研究。

**Method:** 基于Sentinel-2真彩色影像与ESA WorldCover标注构建了BELDE数据集，包含1,088,385对图像-分割图，空间分辨率10米，覆盖7类地物；并额外构建了BELDE-K（韩国，16,607对）与BELDE-CA-NV（美国加州-内华达，88,155对）以支持跨域泛化评估；采用多种语义分割架构建立基线结果，进行域内与跨域性能评测。

**Result:** 在BELDE欧洲测试集上，模型F1得分达83.0%；在BELDE-CA-NV和BELDE-K上分别降至66.4%和58.3%，表明存在显著的地理分布偏移问题，跨域泛化性能有待提升。

**Conclusion:** BELDE作为目前最大的公开RGB遥感土地覆盖分割数据集之一，为欧亚美三洲区域提供了系统性的跨域评估基准，其基线结果揭示了地理域偏移对模型泛化能力的严重影响，有助于推动鲁棒且可迁移的地球观测模型研究。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Earth observation imagery plays a critical role in environmental monitoring, urban planning, disaster assessment, and climate analysis. While multi-spectral sensors are increasingly available, true-color (RGB) imagery remains widely used due to the power, cost, and deployment constraints of many satellite and aerial platforms. However, existing land-cover segmentation datasets are often limited in geographic coverage, scale, or public accessibility.
  To bridge this gap, we introduce BELDE (Building a Large-scale Earth-observation Land-cover Dataset for Europe), a publicly available dataset tailored for RGB-based remote sensing semantic segmentation. Constructed from Sentinel-2 true-color images and ESA WorldCover data annotations, BELDE contains 1,088,385 curated image-segmentation map pairs spanning Europe with 7 land-cover classes at 10 m spatial resolution, making it one of the largest publicly available RGB land-cover segmentation datasets for Earth observation. To facilitate cross-region generalization studies, we additionally introduce BELDE-K (16,607 pairs) covering the Republic of Korea and BELDE-CA-NV (88,155 pairs) covering California and Nevada in the United States.
  We establish baseline results using multiple semantic segmentation architectures and evaluate both in-domain and cross-domain performance. Models trained on BELDE achieve an F1 score of 83.0% on the European test set, while performance decreases to 66.4% on BELDE-CA-NV and 58.3% on BELDE-K, highlighting the challenges posed by out-of-distribution geographic domain shift. By providing a continental-scale RGB segmentation and evaluation benchmark, BELDE supports the development of robust and transferable Earth observation models. The dataset and benchmark resources will be publicly released.


### [18] [PROTON: Prototype-Based Test-Time Online OOD Detection for Medical VLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20913)
*Abhijit Das, Nichula Wasalathilaka, Yifan Lu, Adinath Dukre, Dwarikanath Mahapatra, Shadab Khan, Imran Razzak*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
PROTON是一种轻量级在线后验模块，通过维护来自高置信度测试预测的原型库并自适应融合原型距离与最大概念匹配（MCM）分数，在不修改模型、无需训练数据或提示工程的前提下，显著提升了医学视觉语言模型在分布外检测任务中（尤其是协变量偏移场景）的性能。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有医学视觉语言模型（VLM）在零样本临床图像分类中无法可靠检测分布外（OOD）输入，且没有任何静态评分方法能在所有偏移类型上均有效：最大概念匹配（MCM）在远域OOD上AUROC达76.4%，但在协变量偏移（如超宽视野眼底图像）上仅42.4%，近乎随机性能。这一性能差距源于结构失配——协变量偏移输入在softmax空间中与分布内样本不可区分，却在VLM嵌入空间中占据不同区域，已有的静态方法未能利用这一未被挖掘的信号。

**Method:** 本文提出PROTON（基于原型的测试时在线OOD检测），一种轻量级后验模块：从高置信度测试预测中在线维护一个原型库，并通过流级方差统计量自适应地将原型距离与MCM评分相融合。该方法无需模型修改、训练数据或提示工程，即可在测试阶段实时运行。

**Result:** 在眼科学基准FLAIR + FIVES上，PROTON相较于MCM在协变量偏移、语义偏移和远域OOD上分别提升了+23.9、+8.8和+8.1 AUROC，成为唯一无需层次化提示或有标签数据即可在三种偏移类型上均实现提升的零样本方法。

**Conclusion:** PROTON通过在线原型库与自适应融合策略有效利用了VLM嵌入空间中协变量偏移样本的结构性差异信号，在无需模型训练或数据标注的条件下实现了全类型OOD检测性能的显著提升，为医学VLM的可靠部署提供了实用且通用的零样本后验解决方案。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Medical vision-language models (VLMs) enable zero-shot clinical image classification, yet reliably detecting out-of-distribution (OOD) inputs at deployment remains an open problem. No static scoring method works across all shift types: Maximum Concept Matching (MCM) on FLAIR achieves 76.4% AUROC for far-OOD but only 42.4% for covariate shifts such as ultra-wide-field fundus images, effectively random. We trace this to a structural mismatch: covariate-shifted inputs are indistinguishable from in-distribution samples in softmax space, yet occupy distinct regions in the VLM embedding space. To exploit this untapped signal, we propose PROTON (PROtotype-based Test-time ONline OOD detection), a lightweight post-hoc module that maintains an online prototype bank from high-confidence test predictions and adaptively fuses prototype distance with MCM scoring via stream-level variance statistics, requiring no model modification, training data, or prompt engineering. On the ophthalmology benchmark FLAIR + FIVES, PROTON improves MCM by +23.9 AUROC on covariate shift, +8.8 on semantic shift, and +8.1 on far-OOD, making it the only zero-shot method to improve all three without hierarchical prompts or labeled data. Code is available at https://github.com/GenMI-Lab/PROTON, and the project page is available at https://genmi-lab.github.io/PROTON.


### [19] [GIM-ENDO: A Multimodal Endoscopic Image and Video Dataset for Gastric Intestinal Metaplasia Morphology and Pathology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20919)
*Mojgan Forootan, Mahziar Setayeshfar, Ali Darvishi, Mohammad Tashakoripour, Hamidreza Bolhasani*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
GIM-ENDO是一个公开可用的、经组织病理学验证的胃黏膜肠上皮化生（GIM）内镜数据集，包含24名患者的白光内镜和图像增强内镜（NBI、M-NBI）影像及详细的GIM亚型、内镜征象和OLGA/OLGIM分期标注，旨在为AI辅助GIM实时检测和表征模型的开发提供标准化基准数据。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 胃黏膜肠上皮化生（GIM）是胃异型增生和腺癌的前驱病变，早期检测对阻断癌变进程至关重要，人工智能在GIM的实时内镜检测和表征方面具有巨大潜力。然而，可靠AI模型的开发一直受限于缺乏公开可用且经组织病理学验证的数据集，该数据集需同时包含详细的内镜标注、组织学亚型（完全型与不完全型）、标准化分级系统和正常黏膜模式，GIM-ENDO数据集正是为填补这一空白而设计。

**Method:** GIM-ENDO数据集采用Olympus EVIS X1系统，通过白光内镜（WLE）和图像增强内镜（IEE，包括窄带成像NBI及放大NBI M-NBI）采集了来自24名患者（22例GIM阳性、2例正常对照）的图像与视频片段，并收集了相关人口学数据、内镜发现、组织病理学结果和幽门螺杆菌状态。在标注方面，数据集涵盖了六种主要IEE内镜征象（浅蓝峰LBC、边缘混浊带MTB、白色不透明物质WOS、TV模式/融合、萎缩和地图状红斑MLE）以及AHP和GA两种额外内镜发现，所有GIM阳性病例均标注了完全型与不完全型亚型，并在有完整组织学取材的情况下提供了OLGA和OLGIM分期信息。

**Result:** 该数据集已公开在Zenodo平台（https://doi.org/10.5281/zenodo.20707267），并设有DataBioX网站（https://databiox.com）提供最新更新信息，相关工作已投稿至MICCAI 2026开放数据赛道。数据集包含完整的影像数据和结构化标注，为AI模型的训练和评估提供了标准化的基准资源。

**Conclusion:** GIM-ENDO数据集通过提供首个经组织病理学验证的、包含详细内镜征象和GIM亚型标注的公开数据集，填补了GIM AI研究领域的关键数据空白，有望推动基于内镜的AI辅助GIM实时检测与分型技术的发展。该数据集的公开共享将促进不同AI模型之间的公平比较与可复现研究，为GIM早期识别和胃癌预防提供重要的数据基础。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Gastric intestinal metaplasia (GIM) is a precursor lesion to gastric dysplasia and adenocarcinoma whose early detection is crucial for intervening in the carcinogenesis cascade. Artificial intelligence (AI) holds considerable promise for real-time endoscopic detection and characterization of GIM. However, development of reliable AI models has been constrained by the absence of publicly available, histopathologically validated datasets that combine detailed endoscopic annotations, histological subtype (complete and incomplete), standardized grading systems, and normal mucosal patterns. GIM-ENDO was designed to fill this gap. The dataset comprises demographic data, endoscopic findings, histopathological results, and H. pylori status acquired using the Olympus EVIS X1 system with white-light endoscopy (WLE) and image-enhanced endoscopy (IEE), including narrow-band imaging (NBI) and magnifying NBI (M-NBI), along with images and video clips from 24 patients (22 GIM-positive, 2 normal controls). Annotations cover six primary IEE endoscopic signs -- light blue crest (LBC), marginal turbid band (MTB), white opaque substance (WOS), TV pattern (Fusion), atrophy, and map-like erythema (MLE) -- plus two additional endoscopic findings (AHP and GA) recorded where present. GIM subtypes (complete and incomplete) are annotated for all GIM-positive cases; OLGA and OLGIM staging are provided where complete histological sampling was available. The dataset is publicly accessible at https://doi.org/10.5281/zenodo.20707267. For the latest updates and further information regarding this dataset, readers are referred to the DataBioX website: https://databiox.com
  A short version of this work has been submitted to MICCAI 2026 Open Data Track.


### [20] [UNITY: Attention Flow Networks for Adaptive Conditioning in Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20971)
*Aryan Das, Koushik Biswas, Moloud Abdar, Vinay Kumar Verma*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
UNITY提出了一种两阶段训练范式（通用阶段+专用阶段），结合可变形注意力流（MAF）网络和Morph Wrapper模块，实现多模态条件扩散图像生成中共享语义与专用特征的统一学习，在保持恒定复杂度的前提下显著降低推理延迟和内存消耗，达到最先进的图像保真度。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有条件扩散图像生成方法通常为每种条件模态（如文本、草图、深度图等）单独训练适配器，忽略了跨模态间的共享语义，导致可扩展性差且资源开销大。UNITY旨在解决多模态条件联合训练中缺乏统一框架的问题，实现高效且可扩展的复合条件生成。

**Method:** UNITY提出两阶段训练范式：通用阶段（Universal Stage）使用一半训练步数联合学习所有条件模态的跨模态共享表征；专用阶段（Specialization Stage）在剩余训练预算内精炼各模态的专有特征。核心模块包括可变形注意力流（MAF）网络和Morph Wrapper模块，通过可学习流场和基于注意力的融合实现通道感知与空间自适应的特征对齐，在单条件和复合条件下均保持恒定复杂度。

**Result:** 在多个数据集上的大量实验表明，UNITY在图像保真度上达到最先进水平，同时在推理延迟和内存消耗方面展现出显著优势，优于分别训练独立适配器的基线方法。

**Conclusion:** UNITY通过统一的多模态适配器框架证明了共享语义学习与专用特征精炼的两阶段策略在扩散模型条件生成中的有效性，为可扩展、资源高效的复合条件图像生成提供了新范式，其恒定复杂度设计在实际部署中具有重要应用价值。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
We introduce UNITY, a Universal-to-Specialized adapter for efficient and scalable composite conditioning in diffusion based image generation. Unlike prior methods that train separate adapters for each conditioning modality, UNITY jointly learns shared semantics across multiple conditioning types and subsequently specializes without modifying the underlying architecture. The proposed two stage training paradigm consists of a Universal Stage that captures cross modal representations across all conditioning modalities using half of the total training steps, followed by a Specialization Stage that refines modality specific features using the remaining training budget. At the core of UNITY are the Morphable Attention Flow (MAF) Network and Morph Wrapper modules, which enable channel aware and spatially adaptive feature alignment through learnable flow fields and attention based fusion. This constant complexity formulation supports flexible operation under both single and composite conditioning settings while significantly reducing inference latency and memory consumption. Extensive experiments across multiple datasets demonstrate that UNITY achieves state of the art image fidelity while maintaining superior memory efficiency. Code: https://github.com/arya-domain/UNITY


### [21] [Robusto-2: Benchmarking Humans & VLMs for Autonomous Driving in Lima & New York City](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20980)
*Adrian Cespedes, Marcelo Chincha, Dunant Cusipuma, Victor Flores-Benites, David Ortega, Arturo Deza*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
通过对比利马和纽约的人类驾驶员与VLM在跨地理分布的驾驶场景VQA任务中的表现，发现人类与VLM回答存在差异但受问题类型调节，且未观察到显著的地理因素影响。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 自动驾驶系统在采用多模态大模型（VLM）作为认知骨干后，在跨地理区域的分布外（OOD）边缘场景中的泛化能力尚未得到充分研究，尤其缺乏人类驾驶员与VLM在全新地理环境下的系统对比分析。

**Method:** 选取利马和纽约两个尚无自动驾驶公司运营的高难度驾驶城市，采集两地行车记录仪视频，采用视觉问答（VQA）范式向人类驾驶员（分别来自利马和纽约）以及VLM提问，问题涵盖事实性、评分、反事实和推理四类，进行全因子实验分析。

**Result:** 人类驾驶员与VLM在回答上存在显著差异，且该差异受问题类型调节；来自不同地区（利马vs纽约）的人类驾驶员回答趋于一致；未发现因地理因素导致的强差异，推测是由于样本的高度分布外特性所致。

**Conclusion:** 研究表明VLM在跨地理OOD驾驶场景下的表现与人类存在系统性偏差，且地理因素对回答的影响不显著，揭示了当前VLM作为自动驾驶认知骨干在泛化能力上的局限性，相关数据集已公开发布。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
As Self-Driving Cars continue to expand internationally and use multi-modal systems such as VLMs as a cognitive backbone for their Action models; how well will these systems generalize in new settings, in particular out-of-distribution (OOD) edge-case scenarios in new geographies? In this paper, we study this open question by providing a full factorial analysis with human drivers of Lima, human drivers from New York City, and VLMs and showing them dashcam footage collected from Lima and New York City -- prompting them with a variety of questions under a Visual Question Answering (VQA) paradigm. In particular, we pick these two cities as they are highly challenging driving locations where no Self-Driving Car company currently operates in, and ask questions that span 4 categories: Factual, Ratings, Counterfactual and Reasoning. We find that Humans and VLMs diverge in their responses -- though this is modulated by the type of questions asked, and that Humans answer similarly independent of where they are from (Lima/NYC). To our surprise, we did not find a strong difference in terms of answers (Humans or VLMs) that was modulated by geography, likely due to their high out-of-distribution nature. Our dataset is available at: https://huggingface.co/datasets/Artificio/robusto-2


### [22] [CheXpercept: A Benchmark for Evaluating Expert-Level Lesion Perception in Chest X-rays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21020)
*Geon Choi, Hangyul Yoon, Nalee Kim, Jeong Yun Jang, Hyunju Shin, Hyunki Park, Sang Hoon Seo, Edward Choi*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
CheXpercept 是一个面向胸部X光片的视觉-语言模型多层级感知基准，通过粗粒度检测、细粒度轮廓评估修正和语义级属性提取三个层次评估模型在临床关键病灶上的感知能力，实验表明现有模型仅在粗粒度层次表现尚可，且医学专用VLM相比通用VLM并无显著优势。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有针对胸部X光片分析中视觉-语言模型的评估主要局限于疾病存在性分类任务，缺乏对视觉定位（visual grounding）能力的检验，无法验证模型是否具备临床可靠性所需的专家级病灶感知能力。

**Method:** 提出了 CheXpercept 基准，包含粗粒度检测、细粒度轮廓评估与修正、语义级属性提取三个递进层次，模拟放射科医生的认知工作流；数据集通过半自动化生成管线结合六位医学专家审查构建，包含来自2,100张CXR的10,400个QA样本，覆盖七种临床关键的心肺病灶。

**Result:** 对14种通用和医学VLM的基准测试结果显示，模型仅在粗粒度层次达到尚可的性能，在更深层的视觉任务上准确率急剧下降；医学VLM相比通用VLM几乎没有感知优势，暴露出当前领域自适应的系统性缺陷。

**Conclusion:** 当前VLM在胸部X光片的深层视觉感知任务上存在显著不足，医学领域专用VLM并未带来预期的感知能力提升，提示需要重新审视领域自适应策略，并推动更具临床可信度的VLM评估范式。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
The evaluation of vision-language models (VLMs) for chest X-ray (CXR) analysis has largely been limited to disease-presence classification without visual grounding. Such evaluations fail to verify the expert-level lesion perception necessary to ensure the clinical reliability of VLMs. To address these limitations, we introduce CheXpercept, a sequential, multi-level perception benchmark that mirrors a radiologist's cognitive workflow across coarse-level detection, fine-level contour evaluation and revision, and semantic-level attribute extraction. To ensure high clinical fidelity at scale, we construct the dataset using a semi-automated generation pipeline paired with a review by six medical experts. CheXpercept contains 10,400 QA items derived from 2,100 CXRs, covering seven clinically critical pulmonary and cardiac lesions. To demonstrate the current landscape of VLM perception, we benchmark 14 general and medical VLMs on CheXpercept. The models achieve adequate performance only at the coarse level, with accuracy degrading precipitously on deeper visual tasks. Notably, medical VLMs show almost no perceptual advantage over their general-domain counterparts, highlighting a systemic flaw in current domain adaptation. The code and dataset will be publicly available.


### [23] [Sparse Point-Guided Fusion of Supervised and Self-Supervised Learning Model for Seaweed Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21026)
*Tatsuya Suzuki, Kazuya Ijuin, Hideki Tomimori, Megumi Chikano, Katsushi Sakai*

#### 🧩 TL;DR

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 蓝碳生态系统是重要的自然碳汇，精确的海藻分类对于海洋数字孪生中的蓝碳量化至关重要，但传统监督学习受限于数据稀缺与领域差异，自监督学习则无法直接分配类别标签，两者均难以应对水下环境的复杂性和海藻物种的多样性。

**Method:** 本文提出两阶段海藻分割技术：第一阶段采用SSL.Prop.（Supervised and Self-supervised Learning Model Propagation），利用监督学习提供初始类别信息与近似位置，引导自监督学习进行精细分割；第二阶段通过MaskFusion（MF）融合实例级掩码以进一步细化分割结果，实现自动类别标签分配并缓解领域差异影响。

**Result:** 在山口县水下图像数据集上的评估显示，完整方法（SSL.Prop.+MF）相较USIS-SAM实现了0.068 mIoU的显著提升，尤其对小尺寸海藻的分割精度改善明显。

**Conclusion:** 该两阶段方法有效结合了监督与自监督学习的优势，在数据稀缺和领域差异条件下实现了高精度海藻分割与自动分类，对改善蓝碳量化与海洋生态系统监测具有重要潜力。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
The ocean plays a critical role in sustainable development, particularly in climate change mitigation. Among marine ecosystems, blue carbon ecosystems are recognized as important natural carbon sinks. In this context, this paper addresses precise seaweed classification for blue carbon quantification in Ocean Digital Twin initiatives. Conventional methods, including supervised learning (limited by data scarcity and domain gaps) and self-supervised learning (unable to assign class labels), struggle with underwater complexities and diverse seaweed species. To overcome this, we propose a novel two-stage seaweed segmentation technique. This technique first utilizes Supervised and Self-supervised Learning Model Propagation (SSL.Prop.), which leverages supervised learning for initial class information and approximate locations, guiding self-supervised learning for detailed, accurate segmentation. Subsequently, MaskFusion (MF) refines these results by merging instance-level masks for highly accurate segmentation. This integrated approach allows automatic class label assignment and mitigates domain gap effects. Specifically, instance segmentation estimates sparse point locations which then guide self-supervised learning for detailed region segmentation. Evaluated with underwater images from Yamaguchi Prefecture, our full proposed method (SSL.Prop.+MF) achieved a 0.068 mIoU improvement over USIS-SAM, demonstrating significant accuracy gains, particularly for small seaweed. This approach demonstrates strong potential for improving blue carbon quantification and marine ecosystem monitoring.


### [24] [SARIF: Segment Anything for Robust Image Forensics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21108)
*Dong-Hyun Moon, Ju-Hyeon Nam, Sang-Chul Lee*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
SARIF 提出一种基于 SAM 的图像伪造定位框架，通过反馈引导掩码解码器、双编码器设计和块级提示机制，实现无需手动输入的自动伪造分割，在跨数据集泛化和鲁棒性上表现优异。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有伪造定位模型在标准基准上表现良好，但面临跨域泛化能力不足和鲁棒性差的问题，难以应对多样化的图像篡改技术和分布偏移。

**Method:** SARIF 框架基于 Segment Anything Model (SAM)，采用反馈引导掩码解码器和双编码器设计，其中一个编码器经过适配以提取伪造特定痕迹，另一个保持冻结以保留通用特征。通过块级提示机制从适配编码器与冻结编码器之间的残差特征中推导伪造特定线索，并与上一轮掩码提示融合，驱动基于反馈的掩码精炼过程，实现无需人工干预的自动伪造区域分割。

**Result:** 在标准伪造定位基准上的大量实验表明，SARIF 在跨数据集平均性能和对常见图像退化的鲁棒性方面均达到较强水平。

**Conclusion:** SARIF 验证了将大规模预训练视觉基础模型（如 SAM）应用于取证场景的有效性，为提升伪造定位模型的跨域泛化能力和鲁棒性提供了新的范式，并展示了无人工提示的自动化伪造分割的可行性。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Image forgery localization remains challenging due to diverse manipulation techniques and distribution shifts. Existing forgery localization models achieve high accuracy on benchmarks but often struggle with cross-domain generalization and robustness. In this paper, we propose SARIF (Segment Anything for Robust Image Forensics), a framework that leverages the Segment Anything Model (SAM), which has a promptable architecture and strong generalization ability. SARIF introduces a feedback-guided mask decoder and a dual-encoder design that extracts forgery-specific information to capture forensic traces while exploiting the SAM architecture. To localize manipulated regions, we design a block-wise prompting mechanism that derives forgery-specific cues from residual features between an adapted encoder and its frozen counterpart. These features are fused with the previous mask prompt to drive a feedback-based mask refinement process, enabling automatic forgery segmentation without manual input. Extensive experiments on standard forgery-localization benchmarks show that SARIF achieves strong average cross-dataset performance and robustness to common image corruptions.


### [25] [ChronoLock: Protecting Videos from Unauthorized Text-to-Video Personalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21146)
*Jiaming He, Jiashu Zhang, Guanyu Hou, Shuhan Ye, Hanwei Zhu, Yi Yu, Xudong Jiang*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
ChronoLock 是首个针对文本到视频扩散模型个性化微调场景的主动保护框架，通过优化时序去噪轨迹上的有界扰动，有效破坏运动学习过程，防止未经授权的视频数据被用于 T2V 个性化训练。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有保护性扰动主要针对图像识别或文本到图像个性化任务设计，仅破坏静态外观特征，无法应对视频个性化中涉及的时序去噪动态，因此存在将视频数据用于未经授权的 T2V 扩散模型微调的数据滥用风险。

**Method:** ChronoLocks 直接针对运动学习过程，通过优化时序去噪轨迹上的有界扰动实现防护；具体包括：利用结合拟合误差、帧间相对去噪关系和相邻帧变化的扩散目标破坏块内时序适应，以及通过放大块间边界不匹配削弱长程运动连续性；并采用变换采样的更新策略增强对常见预处理操作的鲁棒性。

**Result:** 在 UCF Sports 和 HMDB51 数据集上，结合主流 T2V 骨干网络和个性化方案进行的实验表明，ChronoLock 在自动评估指标和人工评估中均有效降低了运动模仿的质量。

**Conclusion:** ChronoLock 填补了视频数据在 T2V 个性化场景下缺乏主动保护机制的空白，为防御基于时序扩散过程的未授权数据利用提供了新思路。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Text-to-video (T2V) diffusion models have made it increasingly easy to synthesize realistic and temporally coherent videos, while recent personalization techniques allow such models to imitate a specific subject, style, or motion pattern from only a few reference clips. This capability creates a new data-misuse risk: videos shared online can be collected and used for unauthorized T2V fine-tuning. Existing protective perturbations are mainly designed for image recognition or text-to-image personalization, and therefore focus on corrupting static appearance cues rather than the temporal denoising dynamics that make video personalization possible. To address this gap, we introduce ChronoLock, the first proactive protection framework that makes released videos difficult to exploit for unauthorized T2V personalization. ChronoLock targets the motion-learning process directly by optimizing bounded perturbations over temporal denoising trajectories. It first disrupts intra-chunk temporal adaptation with a diffusion objective that combines fitting error, frame-relative denoising relations, and adjacent-frame variation, and then enlarges inter-chunk boundary mismatch to weaken long-range motion continuity. Transformation-sampled updates further improve robustness to common preprocessing operations.Experiments on UCF Sports and HMDB51 with popular T2V backbones and personalization scheme show that ChronoLock effectively reduces motion imitation under automatic metrics and human evaluation.


### [26] [Contrastive and Adaptive Multi-modal Masked Autoencoder for Spatial Transcriptomics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21156)
*Joohyeok Kim, Taejin Jeong, Jinyeong Kim, Seong Jae Hwang*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
提出一种基于掩码自编码器（MAE）的跨模态框架，利用少量基因表达锚点（低至10%覆盖率）从H&E组织学图像中准确推断全切片基因表达，将空间转录组预测视为空间插补问题。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有从H&E组织学图像预测基因表达的方法受限于组织形态学本身无法完全解析底层基因表达；同时，完全依赖图像信息存在固有限制，而利用部分基因表达引导预测的范式尚未充分探索如何高效选择与利用基因锚点。

**Method:** 提出基于掩码自编码器（MAE）的跨模态框架CAMMST，将预测任务建模为空间插补问题。包括：(1) 生物显著性评分（bio-saliency score）与学习排序策略（learning-to-rank）自适应识别最具信息量的组织斑点；(2) 选择连续区域作为基因锚点以兼容实际ST硬件；(3) 跨模态联合编码器通过对比学习对齐选定锚点与其对应视觉特征，生成鲁棒的联合表征用于全切片基因表达预测。

**Result:** 所提框架在纯组织学预测和空间插补两种设定下均一致超越现有方法；在无基因锚点时仍能达到更高精度，且仅需10%转录组覆盖率即可表现出色。

**Conclusion:** 证明通过智能选择少量基因锚点并结合跨模态对比学习，可显著提升从组织学图像推断基因表达的准确性与效率，为降低空间转录组实验成本提供了有效途径。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
The high cost of spatial transcriptomics (ST) has driven extensive studies into predicting gene expression directly from H&E histology images. However, this prediction task faces an inherent limitation, as tissue morphology alone provides insufficient information to fully resolve underlying gene expression. To address this limitation, a recent study leverages partial gene expression to guide the prediction process alongside histology images. Building on this paradigm, we approach the prediction task as a spatial imputation problem, employing a Masked Autoencoder (MAE) to utilize a small fraction of gene expression as genetic anchors for inferring whole-slide gene expression profiles. Specifically, we propose a bio-saliency score and a learning-to-rank strategy to adaptively identify the most informative spots within the tissue. Based on these identified spots, our framework selects contiguous regions as genetic anchors to ensure suitability for real-world ST profiling hardware. To effectively leverage these anchors, we design a cross-modal joint encoder that integrates visual and genetic modalities. By aligning the selected anchors with their corresponding visual features via contrastive learning, the encoder generates robust joint representations to accurately predict gene expression across the whole slide. Notably, our framework consistently surpasses existing methods in both histology-only prediction and spatial imputation, achieving superior accuracy even without genetic anchors and further excelling with as little as 10% transcriptomic coverage. Our code is available at https://github.com/Kyyle2114/CAMMST.


### [27] [BadDreamer: Transferable Backdoor Attacks against Video World Models for Autonomous Driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21172)
*Zhe Shuai, Xiaopeng Xie, Yikun Zeng*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
BadDreamer提出了一种针对自动驾驶视频世界模型的传输性时空后门攻击方法，通过毒化模型学习到的转移动态，使模型在物理触发器出现时幻觉出前方道路空旷的未来帧，从而诱使下游规划模块产生不安全的非避让航点预测，揭示了感知到动作管线中表示层面的安全风险。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 自动驾驶视频世界模型在感知到动作管线中用于预测未来场景演化并提供未来感知的时空表示以影响下游轨迹规划，但这类模型在训练阶段的安全风险尚未被充分探索，现有后门攻击主要操控图像标签、提示输出或动作监督，缺乏针对视频世界模型转移动态的攻击方法。

**Method:** BadDreamer是一种传输性时空后门攻击方法，通过构造触发器-擦除序列（trigger-erasure sequences）毒化视频世界模型的学习转移动态，具体使模型在观察到包含黄色外卖骑手的上下文帧后，要求未来帧中该目标被擦除；模型在少量此类序列上微调后学会隐藏的条件关联：物理触发器出现时幻觉出骑手消失、道路空旷的未来，该 corrupted 表示可传输至下游动作模块而无需直接修改轨迹标签。

**Result:** 在代表性开源感知到动作管线上的实验表明，BadDreamer成功在不直接修改轨迹标签的情况下使下游动作模块产生不安全的非避让航点预测，揭示了视频世界模型在生成质量之外的表示层面安全风险。

**Conclusion:** BadDreamer首次揭示了自动驾驶视频世界模型在训练阶段面临的表示层面后门攻击风险，强调了在干净生成质量评估之外还需进行后门感知的有效性验证，为自动驾驶安全研究提供了新的安全维度。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Video world models are increasingly used in autonomous driving to forecast future scene evolution and provide future-aware spatio-temporal representations for downstream action prediction. In perception-to-action pipelines, these representations can directly influence ego-vehicle waypoint planning, making the learned future dynamics a critical security-sensitive component. Despite their promise, the training-time security risks of autonomous-driving video world models remain largely unexplored. We present BadDreamer, a transferable spatio-temporal backdoor attack that targets the perception side of this pipeline. Unlike conventional backdoors that manipulate image labels, prompt outputs, or action supervision, BadDreamer poisons the learned transition dynamics of a video world model. It constructs trigger-erasure sequences in which an oncoming yellow delivery rider is visible in the observed context frames but erased from the future frames. After fine-tuning on a small fraction of such sequences, the compromised world model learns a hidden conditional association: when the physical trigger appears, it hallucinates a future where the rider disappears and the road appears clear. We further show that this corrupted future-aware representation can transfer to the downstream action module without directly modifying ego-trajectory labels, inducing unsafe non-evasive waypoint predictions. Our experiments instantiate this attack on a representative open-source perception-to-action pipeline, revealing a representation-level safety risk in autonomous-driving video world models and highlighting the need for backdoor-aware validation beyond clean generation quality.


### [28] [HERO: Hypothesis-Driven Evidence Retrieval from Omics for Multi-Task Breast Cancer Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21174)
*Xiangyu Li, Ran Su*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
HERO将多组学数据（DNA甲基化和miRNA）作为可检验的形态学假设，通过稀疏通路先验、TF-IDF检索和余弦门控修复机制，在TCGA-BRCA上实现了WSI生物标志物和预后预测的最优结果，同时保证了每一步检索和验证的可审计性。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有基于WSI的多组学预测流程通常将组学数据作为并行特征流或文本上下文使用，而非将其作为显式的检索约束条件，导致模型依赖嵌入级语义匹配且缺乏可审计性；HERO旨在解决这一问题，探索将观察到的组学数据作为可检验的形态学假设。

**Method:** HERO提出了一种闭环架构：首先通过稀疏通路到形态学先验将DNA甲基化和miRNA映射为K维意图向量m（K=16），然后利用TF-IDF在结构化10条标题上检索与终点相关的区域，最后通过余弦门控c=cos(m,v)判断，当c<τc时触发确定性缺陷驱动的修复机制；该方法限制了VLM调用次数，使每一步检索和验证都可被词汇级审计。

**Result:** 在TCGA-BRCA数据集（930张WSI，患者级5折交叉验证）上，HERO在ER、PR、HER2、亚型和风险预测任务中均达到了新的最优性能，全面超越了多模态融合方法和基于VLM的基线方法。

**Conclusion:** HERO证明了将多组学数据作为形态学假设的显式检索约束能够有效提升WSI预测性能，其可审计的词汇级检索验证机制为多模态病理分析提供了新的可靠范式，并且通过减少对嵌入级语义匹配的依赖实现了更高的计算效率。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Matched multi-omics can improve WSI-based biomarker and prognosis prediction, but most existing pipelines use omics as a paral lel feature stream or textual context rather than as an explicit retrieval constraint. HERO asks whether observed omics can be a testable mor phology hypothesis: a sparse pathway-to-morphology prior maps DNA methylation and miRNA into a K-dimensional intent vector m (K=16), TF-IDF retrieval over structured 10 captions selects endpoint-relevant regions, and a cosine gate c=cos(m,v) triggers deterministic deficit driven repair when c<τc. This closed-loop design bounds VLM calls, reduces reliance on embedding-based semantic matching, and makes every retrieval and verification step lexically auditable. On TCGA-BRCA (930WSIs, patient-level 5-fold CV), HERO sets new state-of-the-art across ER, PR, HER2, subtype, and risk prediction, outperforming both multimodal fusion and VLM-based baselines.


### [29] [MEDLAYXPLAIN: Benchmarking the Expert-Lay Gap in Medical Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21194)
*Han Jang, Junhyeok Lee, Songsoo Kim, Chae Young Lim, Hyeonjin Goh, Heeseong Eum, Kyu Sung Choi*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
本文提出MedLayXPlain，首个面向医学影像报告通俗化生成的大规模多模态基准与评估框架，系统性揭示了现有医学视觉语言模型在专家级描述与患者可理解描述之间存在显著差距。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 尽管医学视觉语言模型（Med-VLMs）在专家级表现上已达到高水平，但其生成患者可理解描述的能力尚未被充分探索。随着《21世纪治愈法案》要求患者即时获取影像诊断结果，亟需评估Med-VLMs能否弥合专家与大众之间的语言鸿沟，以支持患者教育和共享决策。

**Method:** 构建MedLayXPlain-122K数据集，包含来自12个公开数据集的8种影像模态的122,789个区域级样本，每个样本配有基于三级UMLS本体体系（7个语义组、43个语义类型、2,411个医学概念）的专家与通俗成对描述。采用分层本体验证精炼（HOVER）三步流水线生成通俗描述，结合患者中心词汇映射、LLM约束重写和跨模型视觉验证以防止幻觉。同时提出MedLayEval，一个轻量级3B评估器（从27B验证器蒸馏），在五个临床属性上评估专家-通俗对齐度。

**Result:** 在MedLayXPlain-122K上对33个VLM进行基准测试发现系统性的专家-通俗差距：医学VLM在专家描述上表现优异但通俗生成能力显著下降，而通用VLM能生成更易理解的语言但缺乏临床精准性，表明现有两类模型均无法满足面向患者的沟通需求。

**Conclusion:** 该研究证实当前医学视觉语言模型和通用视觉语言模型在患者可理解的医学影像描述生成任务上均存在不足，专家-通俗差距是系统性问题，亟需专门的模型设计、训练策略和评估指标来弥合这一鸿沟，从而真正支持临床环境中的患者教育与共享决策。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Medical Vision-Language Models (Med-VLMs) achieve strong expert-level performance, yet their ability to generate patient-accessible descriptions remains underexplored. With the 21st Century Cures Act now mandating immediate patient access to diagnostic imaging results, evaluating whether Med-VLMs can bridge this Expert-Lay Gap is both urgent and clinically consequential for patient education and shared decision-making. To this end, we introduce MedLayXPlain, the first large-scale multimodal benchmark and evaluation framework for Medical Lay Language Generation (MLLG). MedLayXPlain-122K provides 122,789 region-grounded samples across 8 imaging modalities from 12 publicly available source datasets, each comprising a medical image with paired expert and lay captions anchored in a three-level Unified Medical Language System (UMLS) ontology hierarchy spanning 7 semantic groups, 43 semantic types, and 2,411 medical concepts. Lay captions are constructed via Hierarchical Ontology-Verified Refinement (HOVER), a three-step pipeline combining patient-centric vocabulary mapping, LLM-based constrained rewriting, and cross-model visual verification to enforce semantic equivalence while preventing hallucination. We further introduce MedLayEval, a lightweight 3B evaluator distilled from a 27B verifier that scores expert-lay alignment across five clinically grounded attributes, addressing the poor correlation between standard NLG metrics and clinical judgment. Benchmarking 33 VLMs on MedLayXPlain-122K reveals a systematic Expert-Lay Gap: medical VLMs achieve strong expert captioning but suffer significant lay-register degradation, while general-purpose VLMs produce more accessible language yet lack clinical precision, confirming that neither current paradigm adequately serves patient-facing communication.


### [30] [Extraction and Analysis of Multimodal Concepts in Vision Language Models through Sparse Autoencoders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21197)
*Sergio Lanza, Jae Hee Lee, Stefan Wermter*

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有SAE方法仅分别关注文本或视觉概念，忽略了多模态概念，导致对VLM的全面理解受限，且视觉概念描述质量低、模糊不完整，难以有效支撑模型推理分析。

**Method:** 基于SAE构建统一框架，为每个神经元提出候选可解释概念，通过计算概念与数据样本间的余弦相似度得分来评估视觉、文本和多模态概念的对齐程度，从而实现对VLM概念空间的系统性提取与分析。

**Result:** 在LLaVA-NeXT VQA数据集上的实验表明，该框架相比现有SAE方法将视觉概念质量提升最高达45%，同时保持高文本概念质量，并能够系统性地识别多模态概念。

**Conclusion:** 该工作为VLM的概念空间提供了新的见解，建立了区分视觉、文本和多模态概念的结构化方法，有助于更全面地理解VLMs的内部推理机制。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Vision Language Models (VLMs) have demonstrated impressive performance in tasks requiring joint understanding of images and text, such as image captioning and Visual Question Answering (VQA), but our understanding of their internal processes remains limited. Recently, Sparse Autoencoders (SAEs) have emerged as a promising tool to support the interpretation of concepts encoded in VLMs. However, most SAE-based approaches focus only on textual or visual concepts separately, ignoring multimodal concepts.
  This limitation hinders a comprehensive understanding of VLMs, since concepts that integrate both modalities can be misclassified.
  Moreover, previous visual approaches often produce low-quality visual concept descriptions that are vague or incomplete, limiting their usefulness for understanding model reasoning. We propose a framework based on SAEs to extract and analyze visual, textual, and multimodal concepts from VLMs. For each neuron, we propose a candidate human-interpretable concept and compute the alignment between the concept and the dataset samples using cosine similarity scores. Experiments on a VQA dataset (LLaVA-NeXT) demonstrate that our framework improves visual concept quality by up to 45\% compared to existing SAE-based methods, while maintaining high textual concept quality and enabling systematic identification of multimodal concepts. This work contributes new insights into the conceptual space of VLMs, providing a structured approach to distinguish between visual, textual, and multimodal concepts.
  The code is available at https://github.com/PHDLanza/Multidata_SAE


### [31] [Unsupervised Domain Adaptation for Sim-to-Real Object Pose Estimation with Contrastive Alignment and Pseudo-Label Refinement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21287)
*Nidhal Eddine Chenni, Arunkumar Rathinam, Djamila Aouada*

#### 🧩 TL;DR
CAPLR是一种面向无监督域适应的目标姿态估计方法，通过局部化区域的对比对齐和跨域配对策略，实现从仿真到真实环境的鲁棒知识迁移，并在多个基准上取得最先进性能。

---

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 现有的无监督域适应目标姿态估计方法通常依赖全局特征匹配、多阶段大框架或图像翻译管线，这些方法容易忽略特征表示中嵌入的与姿态相关的特定信息，导致域对齐过程中丢失对精确姿态估计至关重要的几何线索。

**Method:** CAPLR包含三个关键组件：(1) 高效跨域配对策略，利用中间特征在无监督条件下识别跨域中姿态相似的图像对；(2) 对比对齐模块，在中间表示和任务特定表示的局部区域执行特征对齐；(3) 一致性驱动的伪标签精化机制，通过鼓励稳定的目标预测来提高伪标签的可靠性。

**Result:** 在多个知名的目标姿态估计基准上，CAPLR在多样化且具有挑战性的场景中均取得了最先进的性能，证明了该方法在实际域适应任务中的有效性和通用性。

**Conclusion:** CAPLR通过聚焦局部区域的姿态敏感特征进行域对齐，有效弥补了现有方法忽视姿态几何信息的不足，为无监督域适应在姿态估计任务中的应用提供了更具鲁棒性和精确性的解决方案。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Unsupervised domain adaptation (UDA) enables robust transfer of knowledge from simulated to real environments while exploiting a subset of unlabeled target data to improve real-world performance. Existing UDA methods for Object pose estimation often rely on global feature matching, multi-stage larger frameworks, or image translation pipelines, which tend to overlook the pose-specific information embedded in feature representations. To bridge this limitation, we introduce CAPLR that targets the adaptation of pose-sensitive features in localized regions, ensuring that domain alignment preserves the geometric cues essential for accurate pose estimation. CAPLR achieves UDA with three key components: (1) Efficient Cross-Domain Pairing strategy leveraging intermediate features to identify pose similar image pairs across domains without supervision; (2) Contrastive Alignment to perform feature alignment at localised regions in both intermediate and task-specific representations; and (3) Consistency-Based Pseudo-Label Refinement to improve reliability by encouraging stable target predictions. Extensive experiments demonstrate that CAPLR achieves state-of-the-art performance across multiple well-known object pose estimation benchmarks featuring diverse and challenging scenarios.


### [32] [LEViL: Label-Efficient Video Learning via Zero-Shot Distillation over VLM-Generated Pseudo-Label Spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21358)
*Aslı Çelik*

#### 🧩 TL;DR

#### 📘 Detailed Summary
**Motivation:** 有监督视频预训练依赖大规模标注源数据集，且预训练有效性受源域与目标域相似度影响，构建针对不同目标域的标注预训练数据集成本高昂且难以扩展。现有方法缺乏既能避免标注依赖又能保留语义可解释性的预训练方案。

**Method:** 提出标签高效视频学习框架，包含两个阶段：预训练阶段利用视觉语言模型（VLM）为无标注视频生成文本描述，构建可解释语义伪标签空间，并通过冻结的视频语言模型对该空间生成零样本软目标分布，使学生视频编码器学习语义丰富的表示；微调阶段采用目标标签集感知微调，结合标注目标视频的监督学习与目标标签集上的零样本蒸馏，保留VLM语义引导的同时适应目标任务。

**Conclusion:** 本文表明，通过VLM驱动的无标注预训练结合目标标签集感知微调，可以无需人工标注源数据即可获得语义丰富的视频表示，有效弥合预训练与下游任务之间的语义鸿沟，为标签高效视频学习提供了一种可扩展的范式。

---

#### 📄 Abstract
Supervised video pretraining is a common transfer learning practice for improving downstream action recognition performance. However, it requires large-scale labeled source datasets, and the effectiveness of the learned initialization is influenced by the similarity between the source and target domains. Constructing such labeled pretraining datasets for different target domains is costly and difficult to scale. To address these limitations, this study proposes a label-efficient video learning framework that combines annotation-free video pretraining with target-label-set-aware fine-tuning. During pretraining, a vision-language model (VLM) generates textual descriptions of unlabeled videos, which are processed to construct an interpretable semantic pseudo-label space. A frozen video-language model then produces zero-shot soft target distributions over this space, allowing a student video encoder to learn semantically rich representations without manual source annotations. During downstream adaptation, target-label-set-aware fine-tuning combines supervised learning from labeled target videos with zero-shot distillation over the actual target label set, helping preserve VLM-derived semantic guidance while adapting the pretrained encoder to the target task. Experiments on UCF101 and HMDB51 show that the proposed framework outperforms the compared semi-supervised video action recognition methods across all evaluated limited-label regimes. Moreover, the annotation-free pretraining stage learns transferable representations that provide an effective initialization for full-data fine-tuning, despite relying on a comparatively modest unlabeled pretraining pool.
